dice is one of the most classic of dice games, as it employs two well known mechanics, that of poker and that of a game of chance. The game is played with 5 pieces of standard six-sided dice. The goal is something similar to poker, which is to roll the best hand or in this case a combination of the five dice.\r\n\r\nPoker dice are dice which, instead of having number pips, have representations of playing cards upon them. Poker dice have six sides. The classic poker dice game is played with 5 dice and two or more players. Each player has a total of 3 rolls and the ability to hold dice in between rolls. The player then removes any dice from the combination which she or he thinks will not fit well in the goal of achieving a poker hand. The removed dice can then be thrown again for a second or third time. Dice which are set aside to be included in the combination are not to be thrown again.\r\n\r\nAfter the three rolls the best hand wins. Neither a \"flush\" nor a \"straight flush\" is a possible hand, due to the lack of suits on the dice. \r\n\r\nThe hands achieved are similar to poker.
